An analysis of the top Guards (1s & 2s) in the 2017 NBA Draft.

A cosine similarity is computed between each prospect and NBA player, using both their per 40 minutes and advanced statistics from their NCAA seasons (collected from sports-reference.com).

The NBA player per 40 minute set is every draft pick's NCAA seasons from the 1993 Draft to the 2016 Draft with a complete seasonal per 40 minutes stat line. The NBA Player advanced set include every draftee from 2011 to 2016 with NCAA data.
